British House of Commons Attends to British Shipping in China; Baldwin Answers Member's Question; Navigation Rights at Lao Yao Under Negotiation 18

(London) The House of Commons today paid considerable attention to British shipping in China. Conservative Party Member of Parliament Malone asked Foreign Secretary Hoare if he had received a report from British Ambassador to China Cadogan regarding China's discriminatory treatment of British ships at the newly opened commercial port of Lao Yao. He also asked if Cadogan, in view of the importance of this seaport and for the sake of Sino-British friendship, had negotiated with the Chinese government to abolish various unequal restrictions imposed on British ships. Prime Minister Baldwin replied that British ships were permitted to trade at Lao Yao under the inland waterway regulations. He had heard that some difficulties had arisen in the implementation of these regulations. The Foreign Office would soon receive a report on this matter, and the British government would give it careful attention. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

Agreement Established Between the United Kingdom and the United States to Jointly Operate Transatlantic Aviation; Operations to Commence Next Summer 19

(Washington) It was learned here today that the United Kingdom and the United States have now established a transatlantic aviation agreement, allowing British aircraft to land in the United States and American aircraft to land in the United Kingdom. British Postmaster General Banks visited President Roosevelt at the White House today and subsequently announced the matter. It is now understood that United Airlines and Imperial Airways are preparing to launch transatlantic air routes in the summer of next year. According to current plans, the air route will pass over Gander, Newfoundland, and the coast of Ireland, but in winter it will fly via Bermuda and the Azores. (National News dispatch, 12th)

British Air Force Commander in Hong Kong; Conferring on Far East Defense 20

(Hong Kong) British Far East Air Force Commander Smith, along with his wife and senior military officer George, arrived in Hong Kong a few days ago. He immediately convened a meeting with British Naval Commander in China Tyrwhitt and British Army Commander in China to discuss the defense of the British forces in the Far East. He will return to Singapore next week. (China United News dispatch, 12th)

Scripps-Howard Newspaper Comments on the Future of Philippine Independence 21

(New York) The Scripps-Howard newspaper commented today on Howard's report on the future of Philippine independence, saying: "A foster daughter who marries off and returns disappointed seeks refuge. Can you close your door to her? The relationship between the United States and the Philippines, although not entirely severed, will inevitably come to this one day." The Philippines, at the cost of losing the U.S. market as the price of its freedom, will eventually fall into commercial collapse and hardship, and internal instability will inevitably lead to foreign aggression. The United States initially hoped to guarantee the independence of the Philippines by treaty, but the political and territorial integrity of China has long been guaranteed by strong powers. What is to be done now? Although the Philippines may not face serious threats, if the United States wants to make a choice between welcoming and rejecting, the nation, like an individual, cannot ignore its moral responsibilities. Therefore, the United States must devise new plans to protect the Philippines from new troubles in the Western Pacific. (National News dispatch, 11th)

Philippine Clipper Arrives at Midway Island 22

Midway Island: The Philippine Clipper arrived here safely from Hawaii at 2:59 PM today, carrying 10,000 pieces of mail and five passengers. It will fly to Wake Island tomorrow morning. (National News dispatch, 11th)

Haikou, Hainan: The large aircraft Philippine Clipper continued its flight here at 6:23 AM this morning to complete the second leg of its scheduled Pacific air route. The aircraft weighs 25 tons and is equipped with four engines. It is a sister aircraft of the China Clipper. It is now flying towards Midway Island, where it will spend the night before flying to Wake Island, Guam, and Manila. (National News dispatch, 11th)

Earthquakes and Floods Cause Disaster in Greece 23

Athens: Earthquakes and floods occurred in central and northern Greece. Lightning struck and killed three people and drowned thousands of sheep. 457 houses were destroyed. Traffic in the disaster area has been cut off. (National News dispatch, 11th)

After the Anglo-French Plan Was Presented, the League of Nations Became Busy Again; Laval and Eden Arrived in Geneva Together; Secret Meeting of the Committee of Eighteen Nations 24

(Geneva) The Committee of Eighteen Nations held a secret meeting today. After listening to the presentations of French Prime Minister Laval and British representative Eden, the meeting was adjourned until tomorrow. The Council of the League of Nations will consider the peace plan agreed upon by the United Kingdom and France in the middle of next week. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) British Minister Without Portfolio Eden, French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval, and Spanish representative and Chairman of the Five-Nation Committee of the Council of the League of Nations Madariaga, arrived here together at 9:40 AM this morning. Laval immediately held talks with the Chairman of the Committee of Eighteen Nations Vasconcelos and the representatives of the Five-Nation Committee, namely Eden, Madariaga, Turkish representative Hüsrev, and Polish representative Komarnicki. Although the Committee of Eighteen Nations is scheduled to meet at 4:15 PM, no decisions will be made to increase sanctions against Italy, especially the embargo on oil, until Italy and Ethiopia have submitted formal responses to the Anglo-French proposal. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) After French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval and British Minister Without Portfolio Eden arrived here this morning, they were advised that the Anglo-French proposals for resolving the Italian-Ethiopian dispute should be submitted to the Council of the League of Nations for discussion, rather than to the Five-Nation Committee. The Council should convene a meeting immediately, as the current situation is important and requires the Council's attention. It is generally believed that all member states, regardless of size, should have the opportunity to express their positions on this matter. Laval did not object to this suggestion and stated that the League of Nations should adopt whatever procedure it deemed appropriate. However, Laval and British Minister Without Portfolio Eden and Spanish representative and Chairman of the Five-Nation Committee Madariaga had already discussed this issue in the car on their way to Geneva and had agreed to convene the Five-Nation Committee. In addition, this correspondent has learned that although there was an important debate at the Committee of Eighteen Nations meeting in the afternoon, the lounge of the League of Nations was still empty this morning, as the main diplomatic activities were taking place in the offices of various national delegations. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Rome) At 5:00 PM today, French Ambassador Chambrun visited Prime Minister Mussolini and presented him with the French text of the Anglo-French plan for resolving the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. Half an hour later, British Ambassador Drummond followed suit and presented the Prime Minister with the English text of the same plan. The three men carefully compared the Anglo-French texts and then held talks. Afterwards, the Italian government issued a communique stating that "the Prime Minister declared to the British and French ambassadors that the cooperation demonstrated by the two governments in the talks in Paris was gratifying and that he would consider the proposals made by the two ambassadors." According to responsible sources, the Anglo-French proposals are technical in nature and will be studied seriously. It will take several days to accomplish this, so the Prime Minister cannot provide an immediate response. Responsible sources also praised the efforts of the United Kingdom and France to mediate the dispute. (Havas dispatch, 11th)

Ethiopian Emperor Rejects the Anglo-French Peace Plan; Laval Explains to Ethiopian Ambassador 25

(Paris) According to news from the town of Zhaoxi, the location of the headquarters of the Northern Ethiopian Army, the Ethiopian Emperor has rejected the peace plan agreed upon by the United Kingdom and France in Paris. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Paris) Ethiopian Ambassador to France Mayang visited French Prime Minister Laval today. Laval explained the Anglo-French peace plan and urged Ethiopia to prioritize peace and maintain a moderate attitude. After returning to his office, the Ethiopian ambassador issued a communique stating that "Ethiopia will firmly reject anything, directly or indirectly, that contains the following, because Italy's unjust aggression against Ethiopia has been solemnly condemned by the Council and the Assembly of the League of Nations: (1) granting any benefits to the aggressor Italy; (2) disregarding the fundamental principles established by the League of Nations, especially the principles of Ethiopia's territorial and political integrity; (3) exerting pressure on a weak country to subject it to the control of a strong government, and this strong government has not ceased to believe that it can safeguard the victory of its ambitions by force, with or without the assistance of the League of Nations." With the publication of this statement, any hope for an early peaceful resolution of the Italian-Ethiopian war has been completely dashed, and the peace plan crafted with great effort by the United Kingdom and France has become worthless paper. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

(Paris) Ethiopian Ambassador to France Mayang met with a Reuters reporter today. When discussing the Anglo-French peace plan, the ambassador firmly stated that if we are ordered to cede territory to Italy, we would rather fight until not a single Ethiopian remains alive than surrender to the aggressor. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

Opposition Voices Inside and Outside the League of Nations Are Incessant; Representatives of Small Countries Are Vigorously Promoting; British and American Congressmen Are Also Criticizing 26

(Geneva) It is generally believed here today that the Anglo-French control of the League of Nations' foreign policy, disregarding the will of small countries, will face a serious test here tomorrow. Representatives of small countries have stated that the recent Anglo-French peace plan for Italy and Ethiopia is tantamount to selling out Ethiopia in order to achieve peace in East Africa. They also stated that after the United Kingdom urged them to participate in the sanctions plan, they endured great sacrifices in order to achieve the realization of collective security. (National News dispatch, 11th)

(Geneva) The recent developments in the Italian-Ethiopian peace situation have caused great unease in all sectors of the League of Nations. Representatives of various small countries have held multiple consultations today. The Turkish representative was particularly active in the League of Nations lounge. The Committee of Eighteen Nations is scheduled to meet at 4:15 PM tomorrow to allow the committee's experts to complete their report and to give French Prime Minister Laval and British Minister Without Portfolio Eden the opportunity to discuss the overall situation with other representatives. According to reliable sources, the French representative has agreed with the British representative's view that discussions on the oil embargo against Italy must proceed. However, while there is still a glimmer of hope for a peaceful resolution of the Italian-Ethiopian war, the implementation date may be postponed. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

(London) The House of Commons expressed concern about the Anglo-French peace plan today and repeatedly questioned Prime Minister Baldwin. Labour Party Dalton asked the Prime Minister to explain this peace plan. Baldwin replied that he had already spoken about it in yesterday's debate. Today, those who are most eager to have the details of the plan published are himself, but this power is not in the hands of the British government, so he cannot release the proposal at this time. Baldwin also stated that we cannot predict whether the Council of the League of Nations' Five-Nation Committee or the Committee of Eighteen Nations will handle this matter before Eden arrives in Geneva. Liberal Party Harris asked the Prime Minister to guarantee that the British government would not approve any solution to the Italian-Ethiopian dispute that violated Ethiopia's territorial integrity or commercial independence without the consent of the Ethiopian government. The Prime Minister replied that Foreign Secretary Hoare had announced the British government's policy on the Italian-Ethiopian dispute on December 5th, stating that any plan resulting from discussions must be acceptable to Italy, Ethiopia, and the League of Nations. Eden also reiterated this policy repeatedly in yesterday's debate. Someone asked if France would provide assistance to British fleets if Italy attacked British fleets. The Prime Minister replied that it would not be in the public interest to release the British and French government documents on this matter at this time. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

(Washington) Senator Borah criticized the Anglo-French peace plan today, saying that the United Kingdom and France will give Mussolini more than he initially asked for. Mussolini will become the most powerful figure in Europe. If such a plan is implemented, the League of Nations will become a tool of imperialism. It is fortunate that the United States has maintained a neutral stance in the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. (Reuters dispatch, 11th)

Egyptian King Orders Restoration of Constitution; Current Government Remains Temporarily 27

Cairo - The cabinet was about to consider resignation today. After being summoned by the Egyptian King, the Prime Minister was ordered to restore the 1923 Constitution, which stipulates a parliamentary system. (National Telegram, December 12)

Cairo - After the Nationalist Party and the Liberal Party formed a unified party, the cabinet resolved today to restore the parliamentary constitution of 1923. Prime Minister Nessim entered the palace this afternoon to meet with the Egyptian King, who granted an edict announcing the restoration of the constitution. This constitution was repealed in 1930. It stipulates a Senate composed of one hundred members, with sixty appointed by the King and forty elected by the people. The House of Representatives has one hundred and fifty members, all elected by the people. The current government will remain in office temporarily, but not until after the general election. The unified party has resolved to accept the treaty drafted in London in 1930, which was previously rejected. The treaty stipulates the independence of Egypt, allowing it to join the League of Nations. Britain is responsible for the defense of Egypt and other matters. The current international situation is particularly tense. The British fleet is docked in Alexandria, and a large number of Italian troops are stationed in Libya. Therefore, the military provisions of the treaty are very important, mainly because the treaty stipulates that British troops stationed in Cairo should be stationed in the Suez Canal area. Due to recent political developments, Britain's position in Egypt is no longer as weak as before. (Reuters Telegram, December 12)

U.S. Representative Presents Three Points Against Japanese Naval Equality; Meeting Still Harmonious; However, UK Announces Shipbuilding in House of Commons 30

(London) Britain and the United States, leading the representatives of seven countries at the Naval Conference, rejected Japan's demand for equality today. The meeting then adjourned until tomorrow. During today's meeting, U.S. Representative Davis presented three reasons for opposing Japan's demands: (1) It would incite naval competition; (2) It would overturn the balance established by the Washington and London treaties; (3) Japan did not take into account the naval needs of other countries. (National Telegram, December 12)

(London) At today's naval conference, the representatives of various countries studied Japan's demand for naval equality, with much criticism. The Japanese chief representative, Nagano, is currently communicating with Tokyo in order to explain Japan's position in detail at tomorrow's meeting. One of the main issues today was how Japan can reconcile its demand for equality with its principle of security equality, which was outlined by the Japanese representative and accepted by other delegations. U.S. Chief Representative Davis strongly opposed Japan's common upper limit proposal, arguing that it would increase rather than decrease the construction of warships and would disregard the true needs of the navy. British First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell also opposed it. Representatives from South Africa, Australia, and Canada supported Monsell's proposal. All discussions have been very amicable so far, and no setbacks have occurred. (Reuters Telegram, December 12)

(London) Financial Secretary to the Admiralty Stanley announced in the House of Commons today that the government has decided to build eight destroyers and one flagship, which will begin construction in the next few months. Plans are also underway to build another seven destroyers and several small warships. (Reuters Telegram, December 11)

Japanese Demand for Equality Acknowledged in Principle, Actual Equality Postponed to a Later Date 31

(London) At this morning's naval conference, the fundamental policy of Japan's common high limit, in other words, naval equality, will once again be the main topic of discussion, as the representatives still require supplementary and detailed explanations of the interpretation made by Japanese Chief Representative General Nagano yesterday. Nagano insisted on Japan's attitude of being able to advocate for a common high limit without any change, which greatly disappointed the conference. The Japanese chief representative declared yesterday that Japan is willing to be equal to the United States and Britain on the lowest possible basis. To achieve this basis, Japan is willing to dismantle its battleships, aircraft carriers, and 10,000-ton cruisers, provided that other major naval powers do the same. Japan is particularly demanding that its navy be equal to the United States and Britain because it is vulnerable to attack. Only this can ensure Japan's safety. Yesterday's meeting lasted two hours and was the subject of intense discussion. The meeting was even adjourned to allow the representatives to discuss Nagano's remarks. The representatives proposed issuing a declaration acknowledging Japan's naval equality in principle, but postponing actual equality to a later date. However, it is not known whether Japan will be satisfied with this. This major issue is now causing anxiety for the other representatives, who are seeking a compromise on Japan's demands, such as whether Japan would accept a two-year shipbuilding program instead of the five-year program proposed by Britain. (Reuters Telegram, December 12)

(London) Japanese Chief Representative General Nagano declared to the Naval Conference today that Japan is willing to reduce its naval tonnage to any level, as long as it is equal to the total tonnage of the United States and Britain. With this statement, Nagano rejected the proposal of the United States and Britain to discuss the number and size of warships of various classes separately. The Japanese representative further stated that if the equal limit is below the existing tonnage, the United States and Britain should dismantle some of their warships. If it is lower than Japan's existing tonnage, Japan is also prepared to dismantle part of its fleet. Japan is unwilling to wait fifteen years to build up to an equal level, as such a restriction would extend the term of the ratio system. Japan is unwilling to publish its construction plans until the conference has decided on the total tonnage of each country and the restrictions on the number and size of warships of various classes. It is understood that Nagano is willing to replace his demand for equality with a ratio of 5:4:4 for Britain, the United States, and Japan, and stated that Japan must wait until the total tonnage has been agreed upon before discussing the restrictions on the number and size of warships of various classes. (National Telegram, December 11)

(London) The First Committee of the Naval Conference held its second meeting at Clarence House today. When the Japanese representative explained the country's proposal in detail, the differences between it and the proposals made by the United States and Britain became increasingly apparent. At that time, although the Japanese representative explained the country's naval needs in detail, it still failed to fully answer the questions raised by the delegations of other countries last night. The Japanese representative first explained the special needs of the country's navy, and presented figures as a basis. Then, from a technical point of view, it detailed the "common upper limit" method and the necessity of abolishing large ships or reducing tonnage. Regarding the balance originally stipulated in the Washington Naval Treaty, the Japanese representative had previously stated that the country's responsibilities in Asia had increased, and now reiterated this statement, saying that the Washington Naval Treaty was established in 1922 based on the situation at that time, and was not a fair way to meet the needs of each naval power, and therefore cannot be considered complete. This observation is still the same today. Regarding the "common upper limit" issue, the Japanese representative stated that the country's existing naval tonnage should be used as the "standard," and the armaments of the major naval powers should be reduced to the same amount. Although some factors should be taken into account geographically, it is not in favor of allowing warships of various countries to differ from each other in quantity or in purely qualitative aspects for strategic reasons. The Japanese representative also believes that all naval powers may as well join the common upper limit agreement, but this is not important. As for whether the tonnage of each country's navy should be reduced to the Japanese naval level within a certain period of time, and how long it should be, it is said that it is currently impossible to provide accurate figures, and no answer has yet been given. Overall, the situation at today's meeting can be described as unremarkable, except that the Japanese representative's speech occasionally encountered difficulties when translated into English and French. It is obvious that the strength of the United States and Britain to resist Japan has become weaker. In addition, the "common upper limit" proposed by Japan also contains a most important issue, namely, whether Japan takes the recognition of naval equality as a prerequisite for the establishment of a naval agreement. The Japanese representative did not explain this point. In short, the future of the Naval Conference depends on how the United States and Britain respond to Japan's demands. (Havas Telegram, December 11)

(Tokyo) The Japanese government submitted its policy of common maximum disarmament to the First Committee on Disarmament for discussion on the 11th. Whether this meeting will be successful or not can be determined in the next two or three days. In view of the serious atmosphere of the disarmament conference, the Japan United Press directly exchanged views with Nagano Plenipotentiary in London via international telephone, inquiring about the Plenipotentiary's views on the conference. The situation of the conversation between the Japan United Press reporter and Nagano Plenipotentiary is briefly recorded below.

Reporter: What is the atmosphere of the meeting and the impression you feel?

Plenipotentiary: The meeting is very calm on the surface and follows the agenda.

Question: When the United States and Japan are in opposition on the issue of common maximum and the meeting is on the verge of a standstill, will the United Kingdom temporarily reserve the discussion of quantitative restrictions and propose the discussion of qualitative restrictions to get through this difficult situation?

Answer: The meeting is in progress, and it is not convenient to express an opinion. However, if the meeting encounters any situation or situation, we are prepared and will not be afraid of it.

Question: Is there an understanding among the countries on the proposal to separate the regulations limiting the use of submarines from the London Treaty and make it an independent agreement?

Answer: In short, this is a question of the use of submarines. Whether France and Italy will participate in this case has not yet been decided. (Dentsu Telegram, December 12)

U.S. Treasury Department Declares Continuation of Silver Policy; This Strategy Demonstrates Global Currency Power; Indirectly Indicates U.S. Influence in the Far East Cannot Be Underestimated; London Silver Market Remains Chaotic; U.S. Only Purchased a Small Amount Yesterday 32

(Washington) Congressional silver advocates today praised the Treasury Department's actions that brought the London silver market to a standstill, as this move showed that the United States controlled the world's basic monetary resources and indirectly indicated the importance of American political power to the Far East. According to sources close to the Pittman Investigating Committee, the Treasury Department's strategy has shown that the United States is capable of eliminating the profits of those who smuggle silver out of China, and said that the United States has 1,000 million yuan in cash and 150 million yuan in silver. Any action will affect countries with gold or silver standards or managed currencies. Senator Thomas's views were similar, believing that although Britain had attracted many countries to form the Gold Pound Group, the United States could still control the world's monetary system. Britain's Gold Pound Group is an organization to counter the United States, but the United States has sufficient resources to absorb gold and silver from all over the world and advocate for stability. Some in diplomatic circles speculate that the United States' demonstration of its power at the opening of the London Naval Conference may be an indirect warning, indicating that although the United States has insufficient troops in the Far East, it also has a strong influence. However, as the price of silver falls, the value of the United States' silver reserves also decreases, with losses reaching 28 million yuan. The most appropriate explanation for the recent drop in silver prices is still as follows: On Tuesday, the London market had 25 million ounces of silver for sale. If the United States purchased all of it, it would first have to purchase 3 million pounds of British gold, fearing that the pound price would rise sharply and affect foreign exchange, so it temporarily stopped purchasing. Today, the Treasury Department still firmly insists that the silver purchase policy has not changed, which is also noteworthy. If it wants to achieve a ratio of three parts gold to one part silver, the United States still needs to purchase 130 million ounces. (National Telegram, December 11)

(London) Londoners believe that the U.S. government suspended the purchase of silver because the Chinese government's decision not to use silver as currency undermined the U.S.'s goal of increasing the purchasing power of the silver group. This is considered a retaliatory action. Senator Thomas, a leader of the silver faction in the U.S. Senate, strongly supports the Treasury Department's remarks on changing the silver purchase policy, which is considered important because the change in this policy will cause the silver price, which the silver faction previously fully supported, to fall. Thomas actually considers the change a good strategy, which is why his remarks are highly valued. The U.S. Treasury Department's actions caused the London silver market to remain chaotic today, unable to settle silver prices normally and promptly. Approximately 6 million ounces of silver were sold, but the U.S. Treasury Department only prepared to purchase 450,000 ounces. As a result, the exchange allocated the amount purchased by the United States to the various sellers. There were fewer sellers of forward silver, knowing that there may not be an opportunity to settle the price of forward silver for a while. However, it is reported that some forward entrustment orders have been changed to spot sales. In the morning, because there was no news of U.S. purchases, the market was chaotic again, but the spot price was finally determined to be 27.5 pence, but only a portion of the sales were transacted. There was no trading in forward silver. Sellers were limited to the amount that the United States was willing to buy. It is estimated that the amount purchased by the United States was only about 7.5% of the sales. After the silver price was listed, there were only sellers and no buyers. (Reuters Telegram, December 11)

(London) The London silver price only stopped falling after the U.S. Treasury Department purchased 500,000 ounces today. However, the amount purchased by the United States was only 7.5% of the total offered before the listing, and was purchased on an average basis based on the amount offered by each party. At the same time, brokers have decided to temporarily suspend trading to wait for the market atmosphere to clear up a bit. Someone intended to organize a banking group to rescue the silver market, but it failed today. The details of the plan could not be confirmed, but according to rumors, banks in the Far East contacted American banks to organize this group. It is also reported that brokers have advised some customers to amend their "sell at market price" entrustments to slightly reduce the current pressure. (National Telegram, December 11)

(London) The U.S. silver policy is extremely confusing. London and New York are both in the dark. According to the Financial Times, Wall Street bankers have no idea about the British Treasury Department's intentions. The U.S. Treasury Department's monetary policy was initially to purchase gold, and then to purchase silver. The results have not disappointed the U.S. Treasury Department, which is probably the real reason for the sudden suspension of the silver purchase policy. The success of the U.S. silver policy is nothing more than disrupting Chinese trade, forcing China to abandon the silver standard, and creating the status of speculators and long positions. If the United States does not purchase, then this long position will not be able to end. The Daily Telegraph reported that although the United States purchased very little silver yesterday, the United States has re-entered the silver market, which is gratifying. The general opinion is that the United States now wants to crack down on speculators. The Financial News stated that the United States wants to force China to restore the silver standard. The United States has the power to force the Chinese government to do so. If the United States does not purchase silver from the Chinese government, it can destroy the Chinese government's recently adopted monetary reform plan, as the Chinese government will not be able to maintain the exchange rate of the currency at the new price. How much will the price of silver have to fall to reach equilibrium? This is the question. (Reuters Telegram, December 12)

(Washington) The U.S. Treasury Department's change in silver strategy has once again led to speculation that the government's silver purchase policy will become an important issue in the Senate after Congress convenes. Senator Thomas stated today that when Congress reconvenes, he will convene silver faction members to examine the entire situation, or ask whether to ask the U.S. Treasury Secretary to explain his actions. Thomas replied, "I do not pay attention to this procedure, because Morgenthau does not need to attend the Senate, nor can he be forced to attend. Even if Morgenthau attends, he does not need to answer any questions." The U.S. Treasury Department is still silent, and New Yorkers are speculating more and more about the silver stalemate. Wall Street operators expressed their opinions, saying that the Treasury Department will still buy silver, but in smaller quantities and at lower prices. At the same time, some people speculate about the possibility of China reconsidering its monetary system plan and still accumulating silver coins. Judging from the current situation, the silver faction in the Senate may continue to fight and force the Treasury Department to express its strategy and opinions, but it is generally believed that the silver faction's actions may not be successful. (Reuters Telegram, December 11)

(Washington) Representative Dice, an active member of the silver faction in the House of Representatives, declared today that he would ask President Roosevelt to implement the silver purchase law to revitalize American exports. The law has a broad meaning and allows the United States to exchange surplus goods for foreign silver, so as to avoid purchasing in the open market and causing the current international unrest. We should clearly tell the world that we only want to purchase the same amount of silver from countries that purchase surplus American goods. If so, we can sell surplus cotton and wheat according to the barter method and prevent speculation and the difficulties encountered in previous silver purchases. According to the current plan, silver merchants use the proceeds from the sale of silver to purchase American securities or engage in speculation, neither of which is beneficial to American export trade. I believe the government will terminate the purchase of silver, but will change the implementation of the plan. If we can accept silver for offsetting accounts, we can avoid the problems caused by the large inflow of gold into the United States. This problem may continue to occur, but it can be avoided by accepting silver. (National Telegram, December 11)

(New York) Forbes, the head of the American Far East Economic Investigation Group, discussed the current silver turmoil with reporters from the Associated Press, saying that his views had been explained in the report submitted by the group after returning to the country earlier this year. Forbes also said that he has not changed his views on American silver policy since submitting the report. Forbes was the Governor of the Philippines. (National Telegram, December 11)

If China and Japan Go to War, Who Will Win? Observations by a Foreign Military Expert 34

(Tokyo) According to sources from Japan, a certain foreign military expert made the following conclusions regarding the question of who would win or lose if China and Japan formally went to war: "The expansion of Japan's military strength is an undeniable fact. In the Pacific Ocean, only the combined forces of the United States and Britain are sufficient to restrain its naval power. However, since China has no navy, the Japanese navy can only pose a limited threat to the coastal provinces of China. As for the Japanese army, although it has 6 million regular troops, the military spending it has spent since preparing to invade China for more than 40 years is inestimable. Although its domestic industry is developed, it is very difficult to obtain raw materials. Even Manchuria, due to local unrest, can only transfer a small part of its troops to attack the Chinese mainland. Moreover, in recent years, in order to dump goods abroad, resources have flowed out, and the country's lifeline has lost a lot. As for Japan's hegemonic behavior, it has long been disfavored by the powers and has reached a state of financial exhaustion. Moreover, China's decisive implementation of the new monetary policy has resulted in sluggish sales of Japanese goods, with losses of no less than tens of millions of yuan. Compared with Japan, China's vast territory, abundant resources, large population, and unexploited resources are far superior in strength. If the country can unite, it will be difficult for Japan to win the invasion of China. It is a pity that there are some shallow and ignorant people who believe that China will definitely lose the Sino-Japanese War, and they deposit cash in Japanese banks. They will regret it in the future. Are you foolish Chinese people? Why don't you wake up?" (China United Press Telegram, December 12)

He will accompany Matsui, the Japanese Kwantung Army Military Liaison Officer, to the front for investigation and to find ways to stop the conflict. (December 12th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Residents from the Zhangbei, Baochang, Guyuan, and Second-Fourth District areas are fleeing to the east station of Zhangjiakou in large numbers, extremely crowded. Men and women are exposed to the wind and cold, a truly miserable sight. (December 12th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) According to Song Zheyuan, after the outbreak of hostilities in the Guyuan area, it has been three days and nights. They are currently in a stalemate. The county town of Baochang was captured because it was only garrisoned by a security force of about one hundred men. The Baochang security force retreated towards Ertai. The puppet troops have a tendency to advance towards Kangbao. The city of Guyuan has been fortified and has a larger number of security forces, so it can hold firm. However, the rear guard troops in Guyuan have also increased. Regarding the Japanese side's representation on this matter, it is a request to station Mongolian security forces in the six counties of Zhangbei, Guyuan, Baochang, Shangdu, Kangbao, and Huade, to manage the twelve banners and four and a half sheep herds in those six counties. However, this is not Inner Mongolian territory. The previous government had agreed to allow Mongolians to graze sheep in the area north of Xilingol League. Therefore, there are horse herds and sheep herds in that area. The Japanese side's opinion is actually a misunderstanding. (December 12th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Zhangjiakou telegram: Baochang is isolated, and contact with Zhanyuan and Zhangbei has been cut off. As of the morning of the 12th, the situation at the front is unclear. Telephone and telegraph communications are completely cut. According to official sources, the city appears to still be in the hands of our security forces. On the night of the 11th, puppet troops of Li Shouxin's unit continued to be reinforced by a large number of cavalry. The situation is quite critical. (December 12th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Zhangjiakou telegram: On the evening of the 11th, approximately one regiment of infantry and several armored vehicles of Li Shouxin's unit arrived in Guyuan from Dolon, and launched a continuous attack. The security forces are calmly resisting. (December 12th Special Dispatch)

Students Across the Country Continue to Oppose North China Autonomy; Guangdong University Students Hold Demonstrations; Wuhan Secondary and Higher Schools Open Joint Meeting 37

(Hong Kong) Zhongshan University students resolved on the 12th: (1) To automatically suspend classes for one week to urge the government to make an early decision on its policy. (2) To telegraph Zou Lu to request the central government to decide on a plan. (3) To request the Southwest to urge the central government to make an early decision on its policy. (4) To send a telegram of comfort to the students detained in North China. (5) To send a telegram to students in North China to persevere to the end. (6) To issue a declaration to the people of the whole country. The entire body then paraded through the city to demonstrate. Those who did not participate were considered traitors. The order was very good. Along the way, they shouted slogans such as "Eliminate traitors," "The people of the whole country should arm themselves," and "Vow to oppose the North China autonomy movement to the death." (December 12th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Students from thirty schools in Wuchang held a rally today. No unexpected incidents occurred during the demonstration. (December 12th Reuters Telegram)

(Guangzhou) Although the weather was very cold today, thousands of students from Zhongshan University held a demonstration against North China autonomy, distributing leaflets and appealing to students in South China to rise up and assist the patriotic movement of students in North China. The large contingent shouted slogans as it passed Shamian. No disturbances occurred during the parade. Several teachers also participated in the parade. (December 12th Reuters Telegram)

(Wuxi) All faculty and staff of the Wuxi Normal School of Jiangsu Province recently telegraphed the Central Party Headquarters, Chairman Lin of the National Government, Premier Jiang of the Executive Yuan, Minister He in Beiping, Director Song, Chairman Shang in Baoding, and various newspapers, stating: "The key areas of Hebei and Chahar are vital to the nation's life and are not allowed to have disguised autonomous organizations that harm national unity and arouse the covetousness of powerful neighbors. We hope that attention will be paid to the true popular will to preserve territorial integrity and sovereign independence. We also ask that any unfavorable treaties with foreign countries be announced to reassure the people of the country." (December 12th Special Dispatch)

Beijing Journalists Association Telegraphed Request to Implement Freedom of the Press, Restore Convenience of Reporting 38

(Nanjing) The Nanjing Journalists Association held its fifth joint meeting of directors and supervisors at 3:00 PM on December 12th. They passed a motion to request the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government to implement freedom of legitimate public opinion, to protect the freedom of journalists, and to restore the convenience of reporting. The original petition is recorded below: "Petition to request the prompt implementation of freedom of legitimate public opinion. We believe that at the Third Plenary Session of the First Central Committee, Central Committee members Zhou Fohai and 55 others proposed to the National Government to issue an order to the whole country to effectively protect legitimate public opinion. The General Assembly passed the original proposal, and the National Government instructed all directly subordinate agencies to forward it to their subordinates for compliance. We see the Central Government's emphasis on public opinion and its great concern for journalists. We are deeply grateful and wish to take this opportunity to offer our views, hoping for your consideration. Since the opening of the Sixth Plenary Session on November 1st, when President Wang was attacked in front of the Central Conference Hall, because the murderer had an organized group and falsely claimed an admission certificate to enter the Central Party Headquarters, a subsequent investigation placed all journalists in a position of suspicion. From party and government agencies to police and soldiers, whenever encountering journalists reporting, they would either respond with harsh words, refuse them outright, or openly mock and humiliate them. Some spoke to vent their feelings, while others felt unbearable insult. Journalism is a legitimate profession, and journalists are also propagandists. The situation is painful. Furthermore, stations, ports, and airports, where journalists used to be able to report freely, have now become fraught with difficulties. Even greeting relatives and friends is often blocked by police officers at the station. We have heard and seen many things in the past month and feel deeply. The above situation is completely contrary to the Central Government's intention to protect legitimate public opinion. Now that the truth of the murder case is gradually becoming clear, and the Central Government is emphasizing public opinion, it does not seem appropriate to treat the good and bad alike, leaving journalists in a state of constant suspicion and subject to unnecessary impolite treatment. We are hereby submitting this petition, asking that you take steps to remedy the situation, both to protect the freedom of journalists and to restore the convenience of reporting. We respectfully request that you instruct all agencies directly under the Central Government to be informed, so that the case of protecting legitimate public opinion can be effectively implemented. This would be a great blessing. Respectfully submitted to the Central Propaganda Department, National Government, by the Nanjing Journalists Association." (December 12th Central News Agency Telegram)

Legislative Yuan Committees Hold Review Meetings Separately; National Budget to be Reviewed at Today's Regular Meeting 39

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan's Legislative, Finance, and Economic Committees all held separate meetings on the 12th to review and revise the Organization Law of the Ministry of Health, budgets of various provinces and cities, and regulations on the control of silkworm egg production. Method for Paying Transportation Fees for Banknotes Agreed Upon by the Ministry of Finance and Ministry of Communications 40

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Communications have agreed on a method for paying transportation fees for banknotes. The Central Bank and the Bank of China will continue to operate as before. The National Goods Bank and the Communications Bank should each be treated the same way as the Central Bank and the Bank of China. (December 12th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Various banks had previously requested the Ministry of Finance to consult with the Ministry of Communications and order the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to waive transportation fees for banknotes. The Ministry of Communications consulted with the Ministry of Finance and formulated a method. The National Goods Bank should be treated the same as the Central Bank, completely free of charge. The Communications Bank should be handled in the same way as the Bank of China, with fees charged. (December 12th Special Dispatch)

Mutinied Security Corps Defeated; Martial Law Lifted in Zunhua and Qian'an Counties 41

(Tianjin) The mutinied security corps of Luan County, in conjunction with bandits from outside the pass, rushed to harass the area of Qian'an Gulutai on the 10th. Martial law was lifted in Zunhua and Qian'an counties. (December 12th Special Dispatch)

Zhang Qun Discusses Future Diplomatic Policy: Seek Self-Preservation Internally, Seek Coexistence Externally; Sino-Japanese Relations Should Seek Overall Adjustment 67

Hankou Dispatch: Zhang Qun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, has been transferred to the position of Minister of Foreign Affairs. On the 10th, Zhang returned to Hubei from Nanjing. On the 11th, he convened a meeting of department heads at the provincial government, expressing his hope that they would continue to diligently carry out their official duties, especially emphasizing joint office work. According to what Zhang said regarding future diplomatic policy, he stated, "I was born and raised in Hubei Province, and Hubei is my hometown. This departure is deeply regrettable. Recalling my service to Hubei Province, now two years, disasters have occurred repeatedly, and the people have not yet recovered. It is due to my lack of virtue that I have been unable to inspire harmony. Fortunately, I have received the generous assistance of the people of the province, which has allowed me to strive to overcome all difficulties. Some of the things I have done have been completed, and some are still awaiting implementation. It is my original intention to always be respectful and dedicated to my homeland, to live in Hubei, die in Hubei, and be buried in Hubei. I will never be fickle. The Central Government has repeatedly ordered me to take charge of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, but I have always declined. This time, with the reorganization of the central leadership, I was ordered to be transferred internally. I am a military man by origin and later engaged in internal affairs. Diplomacy is by no means something I am familiar with, and I dare not take on this important task. However, since I am a party member and not in a private position, I have no choice but to obey the Central Government's orders and reluctantly accept this difficult task. Fortunately, Chairman Chiang has come forward to take responsibility. I will take Chairman Chiang's conclusion on foreign relations, declared at the Fifth Plenary Session last month on the 19th—'Never give up peace as long as there is no complete despair of peace, and never lightly speak of sacrifice as long as the point of ultimate sacrifice has not been reached'—as the guiding principle for handling diplomatic affairs. The current national policy of China is 'seek self-preservation internally, seek coexistence externally,' and diplomatic policy is no exception. China and Japan are connected by race, history, and geography. Both are major powers in East Asia and share the responsibility of maintaining peace in East Asia. Therefore, the general relationship between China and Japan should seek overall adjustment. Even the North China issue should be resolved under unified diplomacy. These are all understandings that both China and Japan should have and should jointly define as national policy." Ambassador to Japan Chiang Tso-pin has been transferred to head internal affairs, and his successor has not yet been determined. Rumors that Chen Yi will be sent to Japan are completely unfounded. As for the news that Japanese Ambassador to China Ariyoshi Akira has been ordered to return home and that the Minister to Belgium, Arita Hachiro, will be sent to China, I have heard something about it, but my consent has not yet been sought. Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Xu Mo and Permanent Vice Minister Tang Youren are both well-versed in diplomacy and are willing to assist me. However, Vice Minister Tang has expressed his intention to retire, which will be discussed after arriving in Nanjing. Mr. Hu Hanmin has been scheduled to return to China next month. Director He Xuechu (Cheng Jun) was delayed in returning to Hubei due to a cold, and there is no talk of other transfers. Minister He Yingqin will not stay in Beiping for long and will soon return to Nanjing," and so on. Zhang has now scheduled a reception for Chinese and foreign friends at the Yanye Bank on the 12th as a farewell. Approximately two hundred people have been invited. Department heads and committee members of the provincial government, as well as various legal entities, have also scheduled farewell dinners for him on the same day. Zhang will still take a flight to Nanjing on the 13th and will assume office on the 14th. (11th)

Wang Kemin Telegraphs Resignation from New Position as Member of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council 73

Former Acting Chairman of the Executive Yuan's Peiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee, Wang Kemin, has been residing in Shanghai since his dismissal. Yesterday, because the Central Government appointed him as a member of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, he telegraphed Chiang to resign. The original text is as follows: To President Chiang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan: According to news reports, I have been appointed as a member of the Hebei-Chahar Government Committee by order of the National Government. Since my resignation in the autumn, I have been recuperating and have not been involved in foreign affairs for a long time. I intend to request permission to resign immediately. I am extremely grateful and await orders, Wang Kemin, bowing.

Ministry of Finance Orders Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to Prevent Rice Merchants from Smuggling Silver Coins 75

The Ministry of Finance yesterday instructed the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, saying that it has been widely publicized that cash should not be used since the implementation of legal tender. Recently, there have been unscrupulous merchants raising prices to buy silver coins, hoping to smuggle them out of the country for profit. (These unscrupulous merchants only care about private interests and disregard the overall situation, and it is hateful that they are willing to break the law. The Ministry has also notified all political, military, police agencies and customs to strictly arrest and punish them according to the law.) It is found that the rice industry often uses the exchange of silver dimes and copper coins as an incidental business. It is inevitable to exchange silver coins, but it should follow the method of exchanging legal tender, and send them to the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Three Banks for exchange of legal tender for use at any time. Private storage is not allowed. However, there are many colleagues in the industry. It is inevitable that some will be confused by private interests and privately store the exchanged silver coins, hoping to sell them, which is an illegal act. The Association should immediately instruct the Rice Industry Association to convene a meeting of all colleagues to discuss and formulate measures to crack down on private hoarding and the sale of silver coins, so as to comply with and emphasize currency policy. The agreed-upon measures should still be submitted to the Ministry for verification. This order.

China Morning Industry Loan Syndicate Achieves Considerable Results This Year; A Total of More Than 1.7 Million Yuan Loaned Out; It is Decided to Increase the Amount and Expand the Loan Area Next Year 76

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate is organized by ten banks, including the Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, Jincheng Bank, China Farmers Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Dalu Bank, Guohua Bank, Xinhua Bank, and the Four-Bank Savings Society. It was established in February of this year. The standing directors are Zou Bingwen of Shanghai, Li Zhongchu of the Bank of Communications, and Wu Kenyuan of Jincheng Bank. The general office is located in the Shanghai Bank of Communications, and the branch offices are in the Jincheng Bank of Beiping in North China, the Bank of Communications of Zhengzhou in Henan, the Shanghai Bank of Xi'an in Shaanxi, and the China Farmers Bank of Hankou in Hubei. The original loan plan for the 24th year of the Republic was 3 million yuan in national currency, including 1.2 million yuan in Shaanxi Province, 900,000 yuan in Henan Province, 500,000 yuan in Hebei Province, and 400,000 yuan in Hubei Province.

This Year's Results

The loans are aimed at cooperatives, with an interest rate of 9% per week. Farmers are guided to organize cooperatives, and the syndicate lends to cooperatives, which in turn lend to farmers. This year's plan is to focus on cotton production and marketing cooperatives in the three regions of Henan, Shaanxi, and Hebei, and lend three types of loans for production, utilization, and marketing. The Shaanxi region is organized by the Shanghai Bank, and 17 production and marketing cooperatives have been established, distributed in Chang'an, Weinan, Lintong, and other counties, making production loans of more than 500,000 yuan. The Henan region is organized by the Bank of Communications, and nine production and marketing cooperatives have been established, distributed in Taikang, Zhangde, Wujin, and Yuncheng in Henan Province, lending only more than 15,000 yuan for utilization loans. The Hebei region is organized by the Jincheng Bank, and 13 cooperatives have been established, distributed in Handan, Anci, and other counties, making production loans of more than 36,000 yuan. According to statistics, there are 29 cooperatives in the three regions, and a total of more than 600,000 yuan has been loaned out for various purposes.

Next Year's Plan

The second phase will be the cotton field transportation and sales loans in the four provinces of Shaanxi, Henan, Hebei, and Shanxi, with a transportation and sales loan of 750,000 yuan in Shaanxi, a transportation and sales loan of 150,000 yuan in Henan, a transportation and sales loan of 110,000 yuan in Shanxi, and a transportation and sales loan of 60,000 yuan in Hebei, totaling 1.07 million yuan. Now, the new flowers in various provinces have long been on the market, and transportation and sales are very busy and will be completed soon. As for the loans for the 24th year of the Republic, they will be completed at the end of this month, and will be completely completed by the end of March next year. Including the previous loans, the total amount of various loans is more than 1.7 million yuan, while the original plan was 3 million yuan. This is because the initial establishment was very cautious, resulting in insufficient amount. However, the results in various regions have been quite effective. The new plan for the 25th year of the Republic will be jointly determined after the end of this year at the board meeting. It is heard that the total amount of loans will be increased again and the loan area will be expanded.

Municipal Land Bureau Urges Collection of Practice Certificates; A Custody Fee Will Be Charged for Those Who Fail to Collect Them After the Deadline 77

The Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau issues land practice certificates in units of maps. After a map of a certain district has been measured, a public notice will be published and certificates will be issued on a regular basis. However, after the owners submit the drawings for signature, the certificates and maps have been prepared early, and there are often delays of many years, and those who do not collect them have accumulated to more than 10,000 sheets. After repeated public notices urging collection, they still do not comply. If a method is not determined, it is feared that the certificates and maps will accumulate more and more, and storage will become an obstacle. Moreover, the new certificates are being rushed to be made at present, and it is planned to completely fill out and issue more than 5,000 copies of land certificates that have not been made in the shortest possible time, in order to clear up the accumulated cases. In the future, the mapping and certificate making should be expedited. If there is not enough time during the day, it will be followed by night. The work is very tense, so the people who come to the bureau to exchange and collect certificates are increasing day by day. All the owners who have not collected their certificates for a long time have heard that the Land Bureau has formulated a method to urge collection within a time limit, and a custody fee will be charged for those who exceed the time limit, in order to crack down on them. It has been submitted to the municipal government for approval, and a public notice will be issued and implemented on an appointed day. The methods proposed by the Bureau are first recorded as follows: (1) People who have submitted the old slips to the Bureau to exchange certificates, hold receipts, and have signed and submitted the drawings to the Bureau for more than three months, their land certificates have been prepared long ago. They are now limited to December 31, 24th year of the Republic, to bring the receipts to the certificate issuance room of the Bureau in Fenglinqiao to collect the certificates. (2) Those who still fail to collect them after the deadline will be charged a custody fee of two cents per certificate per month, which will be collected when they collect the certificates in the future. If it is less than one month, it will be counted as one month.

The Shanghai Provisional Municipal Council held a regular meeting yesterday. Lin Kanghou Discusses Year-End Exchange is a Commercial Habit 81

Insufficient to Prove Financial Panic; Also Not a Special Phenomenon This Year

A reporter from the Guowen News Agency met with Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Shanghai Banking Association, yesterday. According to recent reports in various newspapers in Shanghai, various commercial banks have been exchanging with the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, and it is said that this is due to the year-end being near and financial stress. I believe that this kind of narrative seems too serious. Commercial banks exchanging with state banks at the end of the year happens every year and is not surprising. Moreover, commercial banks also have deposits in state banks during peacetime. It is only natural to withdraw them at this time. According to the commercial habits of banks, every year-end, at the time of settlement, profitable banks should naturally compensate for loss-making banks. Therefore, this kind of exchange is a normal phenomenon and not a special situation at the end of this year, let alone a serious manifestation of commercial panic.

Page 9

London Silver Prices Plummet; Domestic Industry and Commerce Unaffected; Silver Exports Cease; Low Balance Tax Rate; Jianghai Customs Announcement: Confiscation for Smuggling Silver 82

Following the U.S. cessation of silver purchases, the London silver market has plummeted. The Shanghai Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee yesterday morning announced a low balance tax rate. The Jianghai Customs announced the confiscation of silver smuggled abroad. Silver exports from our country have ceased. Details are as follows:

Silver Price Plunge Does Not Affect Us

Following the U.S. government's cessation of silver purchases, the price of silver in the London market plummeted. Trading was suspended at the exchange. A reporter from the "Newspaper Agency" (新聲社) specifically visited Secretary-General Lin of the Shanghai Bankers Association yesterday morning. According to him, since the implementation of the new currency policy, silver can no longer be used, and a standard foreign exchange price has been set. For example, one national currency unit (國幣) is equivalent to one shilling and two and a half pence in British currency. The London market's suffering from the U.S. cessation of silver purchases, causing the silver price to plummet, will not affect our country's industry and commerce, and so on. Also, at 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee announced the balance tax rate as 47.25%, lower than before.

Silver Exports Have Ceased

Since the Ministry of Finance implemented the new currency policy on November 4th, the balance tax rate announced by the Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee has not only been no less than the theoretically required balance tax rate but has sometimes exceeded it. For example, on November 4th, the theoretically taxable balance tax was 56.98%. The balance tax announced on that day was 57.25%. On the 5th, the theoretically taxable amount was 58.05%, and the announced amount was 58.50%. For every hundred yuan exported from Shanghai to London, in addition to bearing the balance tax, freight, and insurance costs, there was also a loss of 27 cents to 1 yuan and 34 cents. Under these normal circumstances, formally exporting silver has become impossible. Therefore, silver exports from our country have ceased.

Shanghai Silver Deposit Report for Last Week

A "Newspaper Agency" (新聲社) reporter learned from banking circles yesterday that the silver reserves in Shanghai last week, as of November 28th of this year, were 8,090,000 taels, 294,540,000 yuan, at a rate of 7.98. As of November 29th of last year, they were 33,430,000 taels, 296,540,000 yuan, at a rate of 7.980. Among the above silver reserves, the deposits in Chinese merchant banks as of November 28th of this year were 5,000,000 taels, 250,440,000 yuan, at a rate of 7.980. As of November 29th of last year, they were 15,130,000 taels, 256,080,000 yuan, at a rate of 7.980.

Customs Announcement: Confiscation for Smuggling

Jianghai Customs Announcement No. 1485 regarding the payment of silver export tax and balance tax for the transportation or carrying of silver wares and silver ornaments abroad states, "According to the order of the Ministry of Finance, 'Merchants transporting or passengers carrying silver wares and silver ornaments out of customs shall pay a silver export tax of 10% ad valorem and a balance tax; violators will be confiscated,' etc." Accordingly, it should be obeyed. All merchants are hereby notified. This announcement is issued on December 11th, 24th year of the Republic of China. Superintendent Tang Haian, Customs Commissioner Ba Runsen.

Two Chambers of Commerce Request the Ministry of Industry to Allocate Funds to Subsidize the Construction of a Chinese Pavilion at the Dutch East Indies Exhibition 87

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce jointly submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating, "Regarding the holding of the Dutch East Indies National Products Exhibition, requesting the allocation of funds to subsidize the construction of a Chinese pavilion." The letter from the Commercial Department of the Ministry of Industry states, "According to the report from the Dutch East Indies Chinese Chamber of Commerce Federation regarding the Singapore Chinese National Products Exhibition this year, which was deeply welcomed by overseas Chinese, the Shanghai National Products Manufacturers Delegation plans to hold a tour exhibition in various parts of Nanyang in April next year to expand the sales of national products in Nanyang. However, this matter requires national product manufacturers to take advantage of their return to China to discuss it. We request that you inform the manufacturers of this matter and instruct them to handle it," etc. The matter concerns the development of trade with Nanyang. Therefore, we especially inform you to investigate and summon various national product manufacturer groups to discuss the matter thoroughly with Consul General Song, etc. In response, the affiliated associations immediately summoned the major factories in Shanghai and discussed it with Consul General Song. As a result, regarding inviting manufacturers to participate in the exhibition, the affiliated associations will schedule a meeting of all manufacturers in Shanghai to organize a solicitation committee to prepare and carry out all matters. However, regarding the cost of building the Chinese pavilion, at a time when Shanghai's industry and commerce are in extreme decline, manufacturers are unable to bear it. It is necessary to sincerely request the government to allocate funds to subsidize it, so as to achieve success," etc., which is recorded in the minutes. The affiliated associations received a letter on November 5th from the Dutch East Indies Chinese Chamber of Commerce Federation, the Dutch East Indies Chinese Importers Association, and the Batavia Chinese Chamber of Commerce Federation, stating that the construction cost of the Chinese pavilion would be the largest expense for this exhibition, and other expenses would also be considerable. Overseas Chinese merchants in Batavia are willing to raise between 1,000 and 3,000 guilders to subsidize part of the expenses of the exhibition. This shows that the associations are extremely enthusiastic about this exhibition. The affiliated associations share the same boat and should work together to handle it. Therefore, this document is submitted to your ministry, hoping that you will investigate the previous situation and quickly approve the allocation of funds to subsidize it, so that the Chinese pavilion at the Dutch East Indies exhibition can start construction as soon as possible and open as scheduled. We await your instructions with great anticipation.

Ministry of Finance Issues Clarification on Stamp Tax Law; Receipts, Passbooks, and Insurance Policies 89

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously summarized and requested instructions from the Ministry of Finance regarding many unresolved issues that various businesses had researched based on actual circumstances since the implementation of the Stamp Tax Law. Now, the Ministry of Finance's approval No. 8058 You states, "A telegram from Jiang on September has been received. Upon investigation: (1) Silver or goods receipts should be stamped by the issuer according to law. If stores provide delivery books or silver books for the convenience of the recipients to stamp or sign, and the stores have already affixed sufficient stamps to the books according to the book regulations, then the recipients do not need to affix stamps individually. (2) Passbooks should be stamped annually with 20 cents according to law. For current deposit passbooks, or passbooks for lump-sum deposits and withdrawals, or lump-sum deposits with periodic interest payments, when the time comes for adding new stamps, the banks can affix the stamps when depositing, withdrawing, or paying interest. For lump-sum deposit passbooks, deposit slips are mostly used, and only 2 cents of stamps are affixed according to item 4 of the tax rate table, and there is no need to add stamps annually, so there is no problem. (3) Regarding insurance policies, according to the explanation of the nature column of item 27 of the Stamp Tax Law tax rate table, if a document insures that a certain fact will not occur regarding a certain matter, stamps should be affixed. When transferring shares or other rights, the documents issued by the transferee to the company, bank, or related third party, such as share transfer certificates, etc., which guarantee that there will be no disputes in the future regarding the transfer, should be handled according to the insurance policy regulations."

Goods Subject to Customs Duties Must Not Be Mailed by Letter; Jianghai Customs Issued an Announcement Yesterday 90

Jianghai Customs issued Announcement No. 1484 regarding the fact that imported goods subject to customs duties must not be mailed by letter: "According to the order of the Inspector General of Customs, 'Goods subject to customs duties, imported by mail from overseas, except for serum and vaccines, must not be mailed by letter but can only be sent by parcel or packed in safety deposit boxes,' etc. Accordingly, it should be obeyed. All merchants are hereby notified. Customs Commissioner Ba Runsen."

Tianjin Port Closed Due to Ice 91

The weather has been unusually cold recently. In North China, ice has formed. The ice layer in Tanggu port is very thick, and ships have difficulty navigating. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Tonghua" steamer telegraphed yesterday, stating that the ship arrived in Tianjin and reached Tanggu Port on the 11th, but there was thick ice, and it was impossible to sail into the Baihe River. Tianjin Port has been frozen and is difficult to navigate. Ships can only load and unload cargo at Tanggu Port. Even foreign ships going to Tianjin must use icebreakers to lead the way. Yingkou is also closed. All ships sailing to Niuzhuang from Shanghai have been rerouted to Yantai and Longkou.

Navigational Announcement No. 211 of the Hydrographic Office of the Navy states: "Live-Fire Shooting Exercises from the 'Haibeigangsha' Lighthouse to the 'Jiangyin' Lightship Section of the Yangtze River Estuary on the East Coast of the Republic of China." Dates: From December 16th to 18th of this year, from 8:00 AM to 2:00 PM daily (dates will be postponed in case of bad weather). Limits: The "Haibeigangsha" lighthouse and the "Jiangyin" departure. Explanation: Live-fire shooting exercises will be held within the above dates and times. Navigation will be prohibited in that section of the river. Note: No further announcements will be made when the exercises begin and end. Related Charts: Hydrographic Charts Nos. 143 and 144 of the Military Headquarters. Originating Agency: Staff Headquarters. Addendum: The directions listed in this navigational announcement are calculated from 0 degrees north, turning clockwise to 359 degrees. However, the direction of lights is calculated from the sea. The distance of the light is based on clear weather. Fog signals are only used in foggy weather and will be described separately if necessary. The depth is recorded according to the benchmark plane used in the largest-scale chart. December 11th, 24th year of the Republic of China.
