Rickshaw Puller License Fee: 20 Cents in National Currency 94

According to the report of the Vehicle Committee to the Board of Directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council, the donation and issuance of new licenses to self-employed rickshaw pullers is progressing smoothly, but it is somewhat slow. 16,000 licenses have been issued, and donations up to the 2nd of this month totaled 5,003. The Rickshaw Special Committee suggested that from January 1st of the following year, self-employed rickshaw pullers should donate and obtain licenses, and from that day onwards, the license fee should be increased from the current 50 cents of the local dollar to 1 yuan. The Board of Directors approved this. The Vehicle Committee also suggested that the new licenses for public rickshaw pullers should be calculated from January 1st of the following year to determine the actual number of pullers, and argued that if the license fee is determined to be 50 cents, this fee should be paid by the mutual aid association to reduce the direct hardship on the pullers. Some said that the original rickshaw puller license fee in the French Concession was only 20 cents in local currency, but others said that the benefits of the Public Concession license were greater. The head of the Donation Office immediately stated that he was ordered by the head of the Finance Office to express his active desire that the Vehicle Committee's budget for 1936 should not exceed the amount spent this year. He also said that if the license fee is reduced to 20 cents, the budget for the following year should be increased by 12,000 yuan. After discussion, the Special Committee suggested to the Council that the new licenses for public rickshaw pullers should be calculated from January 1st of the following year, and the new license fee should be set at 50 cents of the local dollar, to be continued to be paid by the mutual aid association. The Special Committee's suggestion was discussed in detail by the Board of Directors a few days ago. As a result, the license fee was decided to be changed to 20 cents of the local dollar, because it was the general consensus that this fee should be reduced to the lowest limit. With this point amended, the minutes of the Special Committee's meeting were immediately approved by the Board of Directors.

Shanghai Municipal Council Approves Rickshaw Committee's Proposal to Punish Rickshaw Owners for Overcharging Rickshaw Tax 95

The Shanghai Municipal Council held a regular meeting on Wednesday afternoon and adopted the following recommendation from the Special Rickshaw Committee:

"The Special Rickshaw Committee's policy of suspending the license of any owner who overcharges rickshaw rent is hereby approved. The owner's request for appeal should be rejected, and the Rickshaw Committee should be authorized to permanently revoke the license in serious cases. Owners who are only subject to suspension of their licenses should continue to pay the fee in order to enjoy the benefits of this license recorded by the Council."

This matter was first reported by the Rickshaw Committee to the Special Rickshaw Committee on December 2nd. The report stated that there was a sharp wave of opposition to overcharging rickshaw rent in November. This was because the price of silver subsidiary currency increased after the Ministry of Finance promulgated the currency system measures on the 4th of that month. At that time, the Vehicle Committee issued a notice advising rickshaw pullers to pay rickshaw rent in local dollars, and informing them that according to the market price on that day, the highest legal rickshaw rent for half a day (i.e., each shift) was 40 cents in small dollars and 28 copper coins. After this notice was issued, rickshaw pullers reported overcharging. As a result of disciplinary investigations, 92 out of 156 owners were punished, 140 licenses were suspended for one month, and nine licenses were suspended for two months. The Rickshaw Committee strongly argued in its report that if this exploitation continues unabated, those who repeatedly offend should have their licenses revoked, and the authority to handle this should be granted to the Rickshaw Committee. According to the report of the Rickshaw Committee plenary session to the Special Committee, after the Vehicle Committee temporarily suspended several licenses, representatives of the owners came to the meeting to request leniency. They were immediately told that the matter had already been reported and could not be withdrawn, and could only wait for the Council's decision. However, the suspension of licenses could continue to be applied until the date of the Council meeting, that is, between December 6th and 10th. Owners without licenses would not be punished. The Vehicle Committee also promised to convey the owners' opinions to the Special Committee. It was found that each case was carefully considered and often took more than an hour of investigation before a conclusion could be reached. The chairman immediately asked whether there were any obvious violations of the Council's measures among the violators. Mr. Massey said that such things only happened occasionally. He said that under normal circumstances, those who profited from the decline in exchange rates were not the owners and pullers, but the contractors. However, the Bureau could only punish the licensed owners and let them transfer the consequences to the contractors of all sizes. Mr. Zhu Maozhen then said that the plan was to allow owners who overcharged rickshaw rent to voluntarily pay a fine of 10 local dollars per license to offset the overcharge. In other words, if the overcharged rickshaw rent was 180 yuan, the appropriate measure would be to suspend at least 18 licenses. The money paid by the owners would be directly paid to the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association, as it was impossible to return it to the pullers who paid too much rickshaw rent. A member of the Special Committee believed that the Vehicle Committee's plan was feasible, and according to reports, the pullers sometimes said that passengers were becoming increasingly scarce due to the economic downturn, and some were afraid to rent vehicles because they were afraid that the rickshaw fare would not be enough to pay the rent. The head of the Finance and Donation Office suggested that in the future, owners who are punished for overcharging rickshaw rent should have their licenses completely revoked or be required to pay the fee as usual during the suspension period as the price for the Council to record the license. Everyone felt that this measure should be implemented in the future, because it is necessary to have strict measures to completely eliminate the overcharging of rickshaw rent. Therefore, the above-mentioned suggestions were submitted to the Council by the Special Committee for adoption.

City Police Bureau Establishes Police Museum 101

Divided into six major sections to enhance police knowledge. Submitted to the city government for approval to expand in the near future.

Since Cai Jingjun became the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, he has spared no effort in carrying out various public duties. Recently, in order to enable general public security personnel to understand investigation and prevention knowledge, a police museum has been established and will be expanded in the future. According to a reporter from the Riri News Agency, the situation is as follows:

Submitted to the City Government for Approval of Funds to Proceed

In order to enable the police and public security personnel to have the knowledge of identification and strict prevention of crimes, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has set up a room in the Public Security Bureau to prepare for the establishment of a police museum. It had begun to collect illegal and other public security-related items for display in the room. Now, due to economic limitations, it only borrows various confiscated stolen weapons, highly toxic drugs, and all other illegal items from the Municipal Garrison Headquarters, the Municipal Security Office, and the First and Second Special District Courts. The bureau plans to expand it in the near future, and the plan has been submitted to the municipal government for approval of funds to proceed.

Exhibition Content Divided into Six Parts

The museum can now be divided into six parts: (1) Highly toxic drugs, such as large and small red pills, morphine, opium, etc., and equipment models for manufacturing red pills and morphine; (2) Burglary tools, such as real and fake handguns, iron hooks, rope ladders, and various iron tools; (3) Counterfeit banknote samples, with samples of various counterfeit banknotes and models for manufacturing counterfeit banknotes; (4) Police uniforms, with uniforms worn by officers and police officers on display for identification; (5) Scientific investigation, using scientific methods to study the order of bullet firing and the footprints of criminals; (6) Crime statistics.

Beating a Three-Year-Old Adopted Son to Death, a Woman Held for Sentencing, Sentence to be pronounced this Saturday 104

Wang Awei, from Zhejiang Shanhua County, makes a living by selling beef sauce chicken, etc. His wife, Cao, 39 years old, lives with him at No. 423, Weihawei Road. They have a son and a daughter, both of whom are young. Unfortunately, the boy suddenly fell ill and died. Jin Guangyu, a ledger room manager on the street, who was a close neighbor of Cao, felt injustice and reported it to the Chengdu Road Police Station in charge. The Chinese and foreign detectives sent to investigate found that it was true. They arrested Wang Cao and sent Lai Fa to Baolong Hospital. Because he was seriously injured, medical treatment was ineffective, and he died the next day. The body was sent to the mortuary. The prosecutor of the Special Court had already examined and determined that Lai Fa had indeed been beaten to death before his death. Wang Cao was suspected of committing a crime, and the police station filed a lawsuit with the court. Yesterday morning, the police station escorted Wang Cao to the Criminal Court Eight of the First Special Court and formally filed a lawsuit against her for the crime of causing death by injury under Article 277, Section 2 of the Criminal Law. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stood up and stated the case, saying that according to the report of the forensic doctor, it was found that the legs of the young child Lai Fa were swollen and had blood clots, and there were seven or eight wounds on his buttocks. There was skin peeling on the top of his head, and there were five or six wounds. There were six or seven wounds on his cheekbones, and there were wounds on both wrists and arms. Overall, there were many wounds on his body, which were caused by continuous blunt instrument injuries and wounds. He was indeed beaten to death before his death. Therefore, the defendant in this case should be held criminally liable and requested to be punished according to the law. When questioned, the defendant Wang Cao confessed that Lai Fa was indeed the son she adopted and that she had not abused him on weekdays. Although she had beaten him once, it was just a trivial matter. This time, Lai Fa suddenly fell ill, and it seemed that he was frightened. Because the family was poor and unable to afford medical treatment, she used ginger and aged wine instead. She did scratch his whole body, but it was not intentional. She also hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend her and asked for leniency. Judge Liu Yugui declared that the debate in this case was concluded and scheduled the sentence to be pronounced on Saturday of this week. Wang Cao was sent back to custody.

Kidnapped Once

Sister and Brother Studying Together

Younger Brother Kidnapped

The World is Getting Worse and Human Relations are Changing, Gongshun Caim Poisoned His Brother, ShunCai Was Furious That His Eldest Brother and Youngest Brother Had Both Married. He Hated His Widowhood and Took the Opportunity to Kill His Brother with Arsenic 113

Shunxiang has married Xia, and also rents a three-story loft in the shop. Living together also include the old mother Xue Xie, and the third brother Shunxi, Recently, ShunCai, because he is twenty-two years old and still a widower, Shunxi is younger than him, the old mother and brother have already booked a marriage in their hometown, and the wedding is coming soon, they inevitably feel inferior, so they repeatedly quarreled with their mother and brother, resulting in increasingly bad feelings between flesh and blood, On the 4th of this month, Xie took her youngest son Shunxi back to her hometown to complete the wedding, ShunCai felt even more frustrated, and often took the opportunity to clash with his brother and sister-in-law, Since Xiang suddenly suffered from foot disease, he could not move and was bedridden all day, and his wife Xia was in confinement during childbirth, so he had to let ShunCai roar. Until the evening of the 8th, Shunxiang was thirsty and wanted to drink, and no one on the bedside was able to serve him, so he called ShunCai to fetch tea to quench his thirst, ShunCai saw that he did not care about brotherly love, recognized that the opportunity had come, One, and responded loudly, and on the other hand, went to the nearby Songlintang pharmacy, bought a little arsenic with four copper coins, brought it back and put it in the tea bowl, and gave it to his brother to drink it all, There were no abnormalities at the time, and they slept peacefully with each other, Until dawn on the 9th, Xia woke up from a yellow beam dream and saw her husband lying stiff and unable to move, calling him unresponsive, greatly frightened and cried, People in the barbershop heard the sound and gathered together, Seeing this state, they rushed to report to the Jiaxing Road Police Station, which sent detective Zhou Yushan to investigate and found that Xue ShunCai was highly suspected, and immediately arrested him, Then Shunxiang was sent to Tongren Hospital by car for treatment, but it was ineffective and he died the day before yesterday. Zhou Detective sent the body to the Ferran Road Mortuary, Yesterday morning, he reported to the First Special District Court to send Prosecutor Tang to the institute for inspection. The deceased's mother Xue Xie heard the news in her hometown and came to Shanghai overnight, However, the deceased's wife Xue Xia could not leave the bed because she had just given birth, so Xie arrived in court and wept, and the murderer Xue ShunCai also confessed to poisoning his brother without hesitation, After Tang finished his examination, he instructed the body to be dissected and allowed Xue Xie to inspect the scene during the dissection, After the dissection, hand it over to Ms. for collection and coffin, As for Xue ShunCai, he has been interrogated by Judge Jiang Shuzi yesterday morning and ordered to be imprisoned, waiting for the police to file a lawsuit and investigate.

Chengyu Store Accused of Tax Evasion 120

The Chengyu Store, located at No. 49-51, Bali Bridge Road (i.e., West Xinqiao Street), French Concession, and opened by Liu Yushan from Sichuan, specializes in selling local products from Western Sichuan. Recently, the store sold a kind of Jintang cigar, a local product of Sichuan. The transported Shanghai selling cigar is similar to the popular Small Green Tree brand on the market, but slightly shorter, with 100 cigars per box. Because the store did not report to the Tobacco Inspection Office of the Ministry of Finance for tax payment and purchase of stamps, it was discovered by the Tobacco Inspection Office of the French Concession. The store was accused of privately selling unreported and untaxed cigars, which is in violation of the relevant regulations. The Western Detective Wu Yaoou (transliteration) led Chinese Detectives Zhou Baosheng, Zhu Qiming, and Zhao Chengen to search the store. Two hundred and eighty boxes of Jintang cigars were confiscated, and account books were found recording that 12 boxes, each containing 2,800 cigars, totaling 33,600 cigars, were shipped from Sichuan. 5,900 cigars were sold, and 27,600 cigars were in stock. The cigars and account books were taken back and sent to the Criminal Eighth Court of the Second Special District Court yesterday. Yuan Jiahuan, a lawyer from the Police Department, explained the case and filed a lawsuit based on the tobacco tax evasion penalty rules (punishment ranging from one to thirty times the tax due). The defendant, store owner Liu Yushan, was represented by manager Wang Zhen (from Sichuan). After Judge Sun Pengxian conducted a preliminary hearing, he ordered that Liu Yushan of Chengyu Store be summoned to court for further questioning on the 16th because the store owner had not arrived.

A Record of Visiting the Watson Electric Appliance Factory 128

— Huang Jiping

Introduction

We are already quite familiar with the term "electric world." Some people say that the industries of European, American, and Japanese powers can prosper, mostly because the electrical industry has reached a stage of full development. It can be seen that "electricity and industry" are inseparable. To expand on this, electricity is the mother of all construction industries. If we acknowledge this, we think of China's electrical industry. Unfortunately, China is too backward. Except for a small number of machine industries using electricity, most handicraft industries are still struggling with human and animal power? And are not all electrical appliances sourced from abroad? In recent years, several commercial electrical factories have been working hard to regain some of the lost rights. Among them, "Watson" is the giant. In order to make the Chinese people understand its contents, this newspaper specially sent reporters to visit and introduce Watson's details as follows:

(1) The Process of Visiting Watson

First, this newspaper agreed with Mr. Ye Youcai on the morning of the 9th of this month for a visit. When the time came, the reporter and Mr. Jin Huating drove to the Watson General Management Office on Fujian Road. It was learned that Mr. Ye had gone out for urgent business and specially sent Mr. Lu Zhongxian and Mr. Xu Qiaoqi to receive us. It is said that Watson has six branch factories in Shanghai and four branch factories in Nanxiang. Shanghai focuses on manufacturing electric fans. The Nanxiang branch factories manufacture all kinds of electrical appliances. Due to time constraints, we decided to visit the first factory (old factory) and the second factory (new factory) on Zhoujiazui Road first, and then go to Nanxiang. After the plan was set, the four of us set off in two cars. After visiting the two factories, it was already past 12 o'clock, and we drove to Nanxiang. We first had lunch at the electrical appliance company, which is named "Shengming" and is also operated by Watson. During the meal, most of the conversations were about Watson's past and present goodness. After the meal, we continued to visit the four branch factories until 3:30 pm before returning to Shanghai in the same car. What excited us most was that Watson, which has been around for twenty years, has expanded from a small workshop with a capital of 100,000 yuan to ten branch factories with a capital of 1.5 million yuan. The products have increased from meters to various electrical appliances. The sales channels have expanded from Shanghai to the whole country and the South Seas Islands. The number of employees has increased from a dozen to more than 500. In China, which is plagued by internal and external troubles, it has developed to such an extent that we cannot but admire the talents, cooperative spirit, and hard work of Mr. Ye Youcai, Yuan Zongyao, and Yang Jichuan.

(2) A Brief History of the Watson Electric Appliance Factory

In the fifth year of the Republic of China, Mr. Ye Youcai, Yuan Zongyao, and Yang Jichuan witnessed the influx of foreign goods and the outflow of interests, amounting to hundreds of millions of dollars. They deeply felt pain and determined to abandon their original professions, sacrifice their personal rights, explore electrical science, and study the electrical appliance industry. They resolutely initiated preparations, setting up in several pawnshops next to Henghama Bridge on North Sichuan Road, hiring six or seven workers, slightly specializing in organization, and naming it Watson Electric Appliance Factory. Specializing in the manufacture of small electrical appliances, such as limit meters, ammeters, voltmeters, and various switches. At that time, there were no technical talents, so they all operated in person. In less than half a year, the sales of products gradually developed. So they added a mother machine, increased workers, and moved to Zhaofeng Road. The scope was slightly larger, so they added the manufacture of generators. Because the products were of good quality, they were well received by the society. In the eighth year of the Republic of China, they built their own factory building on Zhoujiazui Road and purchased important mother machines from foreign countries. By the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the number of workers had increased to more than 300, and more than 100 machines had been added. They strived for perfection internally and added the manufacture of various electric fans, which were sold at home and abroad, and developed day by day. In the eighteenth year, the scientific management method was adopted. In the twentieth year, more than 100 acres of land were purchased in Zhenru, in order to build the main factory, open the Watson New Village, workers' residences, public auditoriums, clubs, and cooperatives. In the twenty-second year, electrical factories, motor factories, screw factories, and iron foundries were established in Nanxiang. In the twenty-third year, the general management office was established and moved to Fujian Road. The internal organization was divided into departments, each in charge of its own affairs and performing its own duties. This is a summary of Watson's history of twenty years.

(3) The Output of Each Factory

Watson Electric Appliance Factory is divided into six factories in Shanghai: two on Zhoujiazui Road, one on Zhongshan Road, one on Kangnaot Road, one on Xiaoshadu Road, and one on Binlang Road. The above six factories completely manufacture electric fans—ceiling fans and desk fans. These two types of electric fans can produce 200 units a day. In Nanxiang, it is divided into four factories: (1) Substation type, box type, vehicle type, and table type (four types) transformers, meters, circuit breakers, lightning arresters, welding machines, and household electrical appliances. In recent years, many factories across the country have ordered electrical appliances and railway bureaus have ordered train fans in large numbers. (2) Huacheng Motor Factory specializes in manufacturing generators, with the smallest horsepower ranging from one-quarter horsepower to fifty horsepower and one hundred horsepower. There are AC generators, DC generators, and magnetic generators. Ten generators can be manufactured every day. In the past, Chinese people could not manufacture them themselves, and they all relied on foreign goods, which were priced expensively and difficult to purchase. Since Watson manufactured them themselves, the sales of foreign goods have gradually decreased, and the pricing has been reduced by nearly half. Moreover, Chinese people can now manufacture motors, and Watson is not the only one. (3) Liancheng Screw Factory specializes in manufacturing various copper and iron machine screws, and provides custom manufacturing of various sizes. It is said that 200 barrels of goods can be shipped every day. (4) Hualian Iron Foundry. (5) Shengming Electric Factory, which supplies electricity to the above four factories.

(4) The Raw Materials and Manufacturing Method of Electric Fans

When we were at the two branch factories on Zhoujiazui Road, we carefully studied the method of manufacturing electric fans and learned that the success of an electric fan requires eleven projects and more than 500 procedures. For example, for copper blades, the whole piece of copper sheet is first divided into strips, made into blades, polished, polished, sprayed with paint, painted, waxed, and then assembled, at least more than ten procedures. Therefore, both ceiling fans and desk fans must go through eleven projects: (1) mold making (2) punching (3) stamping shell (4) suction iron (5) painting (6) winding wire (7) ceiling installation (8) table installation (9) fan cover (10) motor head (11) wooden leaves. This is like a grain of rice. You don't know how much sweat and blood you have to shed to grow it. Now when we mention the four words "Watson Electric Fan", we all admit that it is a high-quality domestic product, and the products are indeed excellent. Its electric fans are divided into three grades: fastest, second fastest, and slowest. There are 56-inch and 36-inch four-blade AC and DC ceiling fans, 36-inch three-blade ceiling fans, and 12-inch and 16-inch AC and DC table and wall dual-purpose oscillating fans. According to the explanation, there are two new products next year, which are the latest invention of the Chinese people and have obtained a five-year patent from the Ministry of Industry. (1) A new type of ceiling fan that blows wind horizontally, so that the surrounding area under the ceiling fan has a cool breeze blowing on the face; (2) A new type of desk fan that becomes a four-sided rotating type; Compared with the current angular three-sided fan, there is naturally significant progress. As for the raw materials of electric fans, Watson gives priority to using domestic products. If they have to use foreign products, they only buy raw materials and manufacture them completely themselves. For example, the leaf board of ceiling fans is only available in Finland. The wire ball and coil are from the United Kingdom and Germany. The copper leaves of table fans are also British goods. In addition, iron, paint, and wool are domestic products, so electric fans are still considered second-class domestic products.

(5) The Training and Treatment of Employees

The Watson factory has about 100 staff members and more than 400 workers. Since the implementation of scientific management in the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, the staff and workers have been united and working hard to produce. The Nanxiang branch factory pays more attention to training. For example, there are morning exercises in the morning, amateur sports and fire protection group training, evening schools at night, and lectures on electricity from time to time. They all feel very happy spiritually. The worker's residence next to the factory can also accommodate family members, and the monthly fee for food is six and a half yuan per person. The daily life facilities are fairly complete. Generally, the daily wage is at least six cents and up to two yuan. In this period of economic downturn, when there is a trend of salary cuts and wage arrears everywhere, Watson's treatment is indeed rare.

(6) Watson's Path to Success

After visiting Watson, the reporter expressed his admiration for their spirit of cooperation and managing a great undertaking in a very economical way. In addition, I have gained two more insights into China's industry:

First: No matter what industry, whether it is internal or external, as long as you study hard, there is no reason not to succeed. The three founders of "Watson" used to engage in other businesses. Electrical science was not their specialty. They relied entirely on their talent to explore the truth and bury their heads for many years, and finally achieved an immortal career, worthy of the model of young people.

Second: Cooperation is the mother of success and a necessary factor for developing a career. The spirit of cooperation of Mr. Ye, Yuan, and Yang has been the same for twenty years, which is a major reason for Watson's amazing progress. I would like to tell the Chinese people that whether you are studying, governing, working, or doing business, you must have these two spirits, and the country will have hope!

Zhenjiang Fellow Association Starts Recruiting Members 129

Since the Zhenjiang Shanghai Fellow Association has been approved by the party and government organs to prepare for organization, the preparation committee members have been actively planning and sparing no effort. All the rules and regulations and letters of appointment have been ordered and printed separately. The 260th inspection was held at the Issuing Bureau of this bank on December 7, 1935. The inspection results are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 15,772,046 silver yuan, including 14,284,4536 silver yuan notes, and the total amount of reserve fund for the above notes is 15,772,046 silver yuan, including cash reserve of 10,433,766 silver yuan. The guaranteed reserve is converted into 53,338,280 silver yuan. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 586,679.80 yuan. The total amount of customs gold convertible notes reserve is 586,679.80 yuan. The reserve includes standard gold 11,553.55 taels, which is equivalent to 586,679.80 customs gold at a fixed price of 50779. According to Article 21 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve shall be at least 60%, and the remainder shall be guaranteed reserve with legal guarantees. Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kangjia, and Xu Jilong."

Public Concession, November: Overview of Industrial Accidents 133

According to a report from the Public Works Department, the number of industrial and occupational accidents in November of this year has shown a significant increase. The number of accidents in October was 150, but it increased to as many as 188. Among them, 9 people died and 10 women were injured. After detailed investigation of the above cases, factory owners were ordered to make preventative measures in 121 cases. Among the 9 deaths, 1 person was injured by voltage, 1 person died from corrosive chemicals, 2 people were struck and killed by falling objects, and 1 person fell from a high place and died. In terms of industrial categories, the highest number of cases occurred in the machinery and hardware industry, totaling 56 cases. The food and beverage manufacturing industry was second with 21 cases, followed by the weaving industry with 20 cases. The construction and garment industries each had 15 cases, and the printing industry also had 13 cases.

Public Concession Fire Department Report 134

According to a report from the Public Concession Fire Department, in November, the department received 50 fire alarms, 10 of which were false alarms. The property losses within the Public Concession were valued at more than 43,000 yuan, and those in the Special Tax District were valued at approximately 1,300 yuan. The value of property endangered by the fires within the concession was more than 4,676,000 yuan, and in the Special Tax District, it was more than 129,000 yuan. In addition, the department's ambulance team responded to 420 ambulance requests this month, and a total of 412 injured and sick people were transported to various hospitals by ambulance.

Weather Report 141

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 yesterday stated that the Shandong area and the Yellow Sea are cloudy with snow and strong to very strong northwesterly winds. The Yangtze River basin is cloudy and cold, with snowfall in several places and strong northwesterly to northeasterly breezes of varying intensity. The East China Sea and Taiwan are cloudy with rain and very strong north to east seasonal winds. The center of the hurricane reached within about 60 miles of 14 degrees north latitude and 109 degrees east longitude at 6 a.m. and is heading southwest-west. The wind force is unknown. Also, the temperature in this city yesterday afternoon within 24 hours reached a maximum of 33.3 degrees and a minimum of 30.6 degrees. On the same day last year, the maximum was 58.1 degrees and the minimum was 41.7 degrees.

Letters to the Editor 143

To the esteemed editor of Shen Bao, I respectfully write to inform you that while I was traveling in Hangzhou on the ninth, I read in your newspaper's local news column that I was listed as a representative from Singapore attending the Fifth National Congress, which is not true. My return to China this time is purely a personal matter and does not involve any other tasks. My travels are coming to an end, and I will return overseas soon. I dare to request that you correct this based on the facts to avoid any misunderstandings. I respectfully inform you of this and wish you peace. Your humble servant, Zhuang Butang, December 11, 1935, from No. 57 Heping Lane, Baibao Road, North Sichuan Road, this city. To Whom It May Concern, the news report yesterday about a certain foreigner suing me in court is slightly inconsistent with the facts. I have never signed any contract with any foreigner. My defense attorney, lawyer Jin Ximin, stated in court that the cause of the report yesterday is unknown. I am deeply afraid of causing misunderstandings and hope that you will grant a correction. I will be extremely grateful. Respectfully, Zhang Siyun of Hongyu Pharmacy Shanghai Office, December 12.

To Whom It May Concern, I recently read in the news column of your esteemed newspaper that the factory in the back of our company caught fire, which is inconsistent with the facts. At about 7:00 a.m. yesterday, smoke was occasionally seen outside the wall on the second floor of the back door, but there was no fire and it was immediately extinguished without any loss. Our factory has always been on the fourth floor roof, and we have always been careful to keep it clean. There is also no issue of chimneys being old and dilapidated. I am sincerely afraid that the rumors are untrue, so I specially send this letter to inform you and ask you to publish it in the letter to the editor column of your esteemed newspaper for correction. We are extremely grateful. Respectfully, Dachang Xieji Silk and Satin Bureau at the mouth of Xiaodongmen, December 12.

Education News

Chahar Province's County Education Funds for the Past Two Years 144

Chahar Province's county education funds for the past two years (22nd and 23rd years) have been surveyed and statistically analyzed by the province's Department of Education recently. The results are as follows:

(1) The total expenditure of education funds for each county in Chahar Province in the 22nd year was 754,662 yuan. Its distribution was as follows: (A) Education implementation 585,357 yuan (kindergarten 680 yuan, primary school 485,780 yuan, senior primary school 118,209 yuan); (B) Secondary education 65,848 yuan (junior high school 1,200 yuan, normal school 15,858 yuan, various short-term normal schools 35,265 yuan, junior vocational 14,357 yuan); (C) Social education 21,761 yuan (general social education institutions 21,015 yuan, school-style social education institutions 746 yuan); (D) Various special project fees 17,739 yuan; (E) Other 1,398 yuan; (F) Education administration 42,703 yuan.

(2) The total expenditure of education funds for each county in Chahar Province in the 23rd year was 709,063 yuan. Its distribution was as follows: (A) Education implementation 559,623 yuan (kindergarten 300 yuan, primary school 454,614 yuan, junior primary school 104,709 yuan); (B) Secondary education 65,382 yuan (junior high school 1,200 yuan, normal school 15,519 yuan, various short-term normal schools 33,867 yuan, junior vocational 14,796 yuan); (C) Social education 20,863 yuan (general social institutions 20,503 yuan, school or social education institutions 360 yuan); (D) Various special project fees 18,208 yuan; (E) Other 1,383 yuan; (F) Education administration 43,603 yuan.

(Explanation) The largest source of education funds for each county in the province is land tax, 117,584 yuan, followed by grain measure mountain resources tooth tax 31,205 yuan, school land rent 34,936 yuan, land apportionment 38,288 yuan, tooth tax retention 26,084 yuan, ubiquitous donation rent 36,095 yuan, township funds 11,519 yuan, fund interest 11,189 yuan, livestock tax 11,270 yuan, donation surcharge 18,304 yuan, measure donation 25,021 yuan, additional ship grain replacement 28,295 yuan, provincial fixed retention tax 11,369 yuan, industrial rent 10,454 yuan, various primary schools self-collected funds 15,375 yuan, followed by slaughter tax 8,945 yuan, land and house notarization use 8,422 yuan, fur donation 6,620 yuan, marriage medical donation 5,537 yuan, school affairs public welfare donation 8,568 yuan, grass contract stamp fee 4,280 yuan, financial department subsidy 3,014 yuan, county area primary school canal land rent 3,524 yuan, local assistance 2,552 yuan, string ticket surcharge 2,182 yuan, transfer fee 1,882 yuan, miscellaneous fees from county area primary schools 1,520 yuan, local education fee surcharge 800 yuan, accumulated grain charity granary miscellaneous interest 700 yuan, Australian stock dividend 200 yuan, military pay rice discount 186 yuan, other 3,482 yuan, and temporary fee land apportionment 50,550 yuan, township school funds 55,782 yuan, provincial allocation for primary school construction fee 2,000 yuan, district subsidy 2,053 yuan. The total education revenue for the 23rd year also reached several hundred thousand yuan.

Children's Year Implementation Association Actively Promotes Children's Films, Convened Managers of City Cinemas Yesterday, Established Children's Film Promotion Committee 146

The Shanghai Children's Year Implementation Association, in order to promote children's films, convened managers of various cinemas in the city at 2:00 PM yesterday on the second floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA to hold a discussion meeting. A Children's Film Promotion Committee was established to be responsible for planning everything. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives: Members of the Children's Year Implementation Committee Jiang Jianbai, Chen Bai, Hu Shuyi, Xu Gongmei, (Education Bureau) Zhang Binghui, Sun Yongyi, Wang Gang, (Social Bureau) Wu Menggong, (Public Security Bureau) Zhou Guobin, (Health Bureau) Qian Fugong, Zhou Wanghe, (Children's Welfare Association) Chen Tiesheng (Child Care Association) and Lu Shibai of Nanjing, Grand Shanghai, Lido Cinemas, Sun Xiaochang of Jiuxing Grand Theater, Bian Yuying of World Grand Theater, Xu Xinyu of Jincheng Grand Theater, Xu Gongwei of Rongjin Grand Theater, etc. Chairman: Jiang Jianbai. Recorder: Mr. Guo.

Chairman's Report: The meeting was opened by Chairman Jiang Jianbai, who stated that the committee has noted that many of the films shown in the city's general cinemas are not suitable for children to watch. In addition to the passive measure of the Education Bureau issuing a notice to all cinemas to prohibit children under the age of six from entering to watch ordinary films, the active measure should be to specifically show children's films to meet the needs of children. Therefore, it is planned to hold Children's Film Day, but the determination of the date of Children's Film Day, the selection of films, etc., are all to be discussed, so everyone is specially invited here to discuss and proceed together. Then, Xu Gongmei reported on the Japanese Children's Film Day method, and Lu Shibai and others expressed their opinions.

Organization of Special Committee: It was decided to organize the Shanghai Children's Film Promotion Committee to be responsible for handling special matters. Four groups were established: General Affairs Group, Propaganda Group, Investigation Group, and Writing Group. The committee member candidates are as follows: (1) General Affairs Group members Jiang Jianbai, Zhang Binghui, Lin Tannan, Xu Xinyu, Lu Shibai, and Jiang Jianbai was elected as the convener. (2) Propaganda Group members Hu Shuyi, Ma Chonggan, Xu Zexiang, Jiang Xiangqing, Chen Dongbai, and Lu Shibai were elected as the convener. (3) Investigation Group members Bian Yuying, Xu Gongmei, Chen Tiesheng, Sun Ruchang, Liang Ruhai, and Xu Gongmei was elected as the convener. (4) Writing Group members Li Mingwei, Gao Tianqi, Xu Zhuodai, Sun Yongyi, and Sun Yongyi was elected as the convener. (5) Zhang Binghui, Xu Gongmei, and Sun Yongyi were elected as members of the constitution drafting committee, convened by Zhang Binghui, to be completed within two days. (6) Each group is limited to convening a meeting within three days to discuss each group's plans. Other methods regarding Children's Film Day plans to divide into five areas: East, South, West, North, and Central, and the propaganda methods, etc., will be discussed by the promotion committee. The meeting adjourned at about 4:00 PM.

Municipal Museum Ad Hoc Board of Directors Third Meeting 148

The Municipal Museum of this city is constructing a new building in the city center district, which has been fully completed. For the convenience of collecting exhibits, a preparatory office has been set up in the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society on Aimu Yugen Road. The museum's ad hoc board of directors held its third meeting on the afternoon of the 11th (the day before yesterday) at 4:00 PM in the preparatory office. Attendees included Ye Gongchuo, Wu Tiecheng, Liu Yazi, Yu Hongjun, Huang Nihong, Cheng Yansheng, Shen Qia, Dong Dayou, Jiang Xiaojian, Cai Zengji, Liu Haisu, Li Dachao, Xu Naichang, Wu Hufan. Observers included Hu Pianxianchun, Chen Duanzhi, Zheng Shixu, Xu Weinan, etc. The meeting was chaired by Chairman Ye Gongchuo, and Secretary Li Dachao recorded. The meeting was convened as planned. First, the chairman reported on the establishment of the preparatory office and explained the methods for collecting relics, etc. Due to the urgency of time, it had already been printed and distributed to all sectors of society. The chairman then requested that it be revised and approved. Next, the director of the preparatory office reported: (1) Preparatory process: rented one-quarter of the Arts and Crafts Society on November 5, started office on the 16th, inspected the new building on the 19th, drafted methods for collecting exhibits and the museum's regulations from November 20, and started soliciting from all sectors of society from December 5. (2) Preparatory expenses: 2,736 yuan. The original four months have been shortened to three months. Because the office expenses are insufficient, the savings from the salary items will be allocated to cover the expenses. (3) Preparatory office staff: In addition to the director and deputy director, Zheng Shixu, Xu Weinan, and Chen Duanzhi have been requested to be responsible for planning. Xue Baolun and six others have been appointed to be responsible for clerical, accounting, general affairs, and registration matters. Next, the discussion began: (1) Passed the proposal for collecting exhibits, resolved and passed, and sent to the municipal government for approval. (2) Passed the proposal for donating exhibits, resolved and passed, and sent to the municipal government for approval. (3) Passed the proposal for depositing exhibits, resolved and passed, and sent to the municipal government for approval. (4) Passed the proposal for the museum's regulations and organizational system, resolved to amend and pass, and sent to the municipal government for approval. (5) All equipment fees and purchase fees should be allocated by the municipal government immediately to facilitate progress. It was resolved to request the municipal government to allocate them as soon as possible. (6) It was proposed that archeology be temporarily attached to the art department. It was resolved and passed. The meeting adjourned at about 6:00 PM.

Children's Education Novel

Little Men (1) (2) (2) 152

—Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Although Mrs. Jo only said a few words, they all knew the severity of the situation and did as she said as quickly as possible. In less than ten minutes, Mr. Bhaer and Mr. Laurence had reached the woods, and Franz, riding old Untie, galloped into the prairie to search everywhere. Mrs. Jo followed her, while the others waited quietly at home. She rode Rabbit again, running away, still having time to put on a hat or shawl. She heard someone seem to be chasing closely behind, but she didn't say a word until she stopped to listen carefully, and the light from her lamp shone on Dan's face.

"You're here! I want to liberate the guest," she said, as if still wanting him to go back, although she was in desperate need of help at the time.

"I don't want him to go, he and Amy haven't even had dinner yet, my desire to come is stronger than theirs," he said, and took the lamp from her hand, smiling at her, but with a determined spirit in his eyes, making her feel that although he was a child, she also had someone to rely on in times of need.

She jumped down, ordering him to ride Rabbit. He initially asked to walk, but finally had to obey; so the two walked together along the dusty and vibrant path, stopping from time to time to call out, or holding their breath to listen for small voices answering.

Yesterday's China Football Match: You You Heavily Defeats Guanghua; You You's Talented Team Wins 7-2; Luo Douwen Ejected, Guanghua Suffers a Crushing Defeat 154

The China Football Association's Group A match between You You and Guanghua, originally scheduled for the 4th, was postponed due to rain and was held yesterday at 3 PM at Shen Garden on Yanping Road. The weather was cold, and there were few spectators. You You, relying on their talented team, fought to a 1-1 draw in the first half. In the second half, they changed their strategy and had smooth sailing, overwhelming the rising Guanghua team with a score of 6-1. In total, You You triumphed with a score of 7-2.

Xi Qiaosheng Opens the Scoring: At 3 PM sharp, referee Chen Jixiang blew the whistle, and both sides lined up to compete. After the start, You You took the offensive first. Xi Qiaosheng dribbled straight in, Xu Jingcheng intercepted the ball and passed it to the front lines. Hu Youcheng cleverly intercepted the ball halfway, advancing forcefully into Guanghua territory. The ball lingered in front of the goal, but Hu Youcheng, Xi Qiaosheng, and Liu Shizan all missed their shots, which was a pity. Zhong Yongsen invaded from the flank, taking big strides and breaking through three barriers. He then pulled back and took a powerful shot, but it hit the goalpost and bounced back. Xi Qiaosheng calmly caught up and headed the ball in, opening the scoring.

First Half Ends in a Draw: After Guanghua's setback, the entire team gave their all, attacking from the sides, creating waves in front of You You's goal. Wang Caigao was flustered, but fortunately, no shots went in. Xiao Heitan, seeing the Guanghua team disrupting their position, waved his arms and jumped up, rushing to the front lines, recklessly. Qu Aisheng, seeing the situation was not good, rushed up to block him and accidentally collided with Xiao Heitan, causing Heitan to injure his ankle and leave the field. Guanghua took advantage of this opportunity to attack the city. Gu Dingxiang launched an attack from the border and took a long-range shot. Goalkeeper Wang Caigao reached out to save it, but Luo Douwen seized the opportunity and scored, making it a tie. Zhong Yongsen advanced alone, but Shi Cheng was careless and committed a foul, resulting in a penalty kick. Qiaosheng took the penalty kick, but the ball flew over the goal, failing to score. After that, neither side scored, ending the first half 1-1.

Guanghua Team Loses Two More Goals: After the break, they changed sides and fought again. Guanghua's momentum was strong. Xu Jingcheng led the three armies, pressing forward together. Unfortunately, their shooting accuracy was off, turning into wild shots. Seeing the opponent's rampant offense, Qiaosheng didn't dare to linger with the ball and passed it straight to the center. Zhong Shen passed it back and forth, and with long and short passes, they advanced to Guanghua's territory. Xiao Zhong passed again, and he scored again. At this time, Guanghua's main player, Luo Douwen, was injured and left the field, making their situation even more isolated. Qiaosheng took the opportunity to enter, assisted by Shen Boxian, sneaking into Guanghua's territory and scoring again with a long-range shot.

7-2, Guanghua Suffers a Crushing Defeat: Guanghua's wounded soldiers were temporarily without , and dangerous situations arose. Eventually, Xiao Zhong gained an advantage with Shizan's assistance, heading the ball in. Xiao Zhong added the finishing touch, making it a pair. Shen Shiqi was envious, unwilling to fall behind, and scored a goal. This angered Guanghua's main player, Xu Jingcheng, who, seeing their territory being ravaged by You You with almost no defense, took charge in the center, commanding the three armies, and their momentum was indeed revitalized. Xu then broke through three barriers, unstoppable. Wang Caigao was unable to save it, and watched as the ball rolled into the net. Time was up, and the gong was sounded to end the match. You You won a major victory over Guanghua with a score of 7-2. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

You You Lineup

Wang Caigao Chen Zhenxiang Zhu Yunfeng Liang Shutang Wang Zhangbao Shen Shiqi (down) Chen Zhenhe (up) Xi Qiaosheng Zhong Yongsen (down) Hu Youcheng (up) Liu Shi Shen Baigui (up) Zhong Yongsen (up)

Guanghua Lineup

In the fourth set, Weng Mingqi refused to be outdone, using his superb counter-attack skills and clever corner shots to prevent his opponent from making a comeback, easily winning a set. In the first set, Sun Lishi used wonderful topspin smashes to render St. Francis helpless, winning with a score of 3-0. Finally, Cheng Changhan and Zheng Zhenhua of Zhong Fa used their wonderful long-range topspin and short-range pressure skills, both overcoming their opponents with a score of 3-0. The performance in this match was wonderful and won a lot of applause from around. In the end, Zhong Fa won the table tennis championship with a score of 5-2. The results are as follows:

Huxi Guanghua Middle School, Nanyang Model Middle School, and Provincial Shangzhong, in order to increase students' interest in sports and strive for universal sports in each school, have organized a three-school sports association. The association held a preparatory meeting at the beginning of last month in the gymnasium of Provincial Shangzhong. Representatives from each school attended, including Wu Lisheng from Shangzhong, Zhang Wenyuan from Nanyang, and Jiang Jingnan and Jiang Qing from Guanghua. This mini-football is different from the current small rubber ball and is still a novel concept in the country. The association has already set the dimensions and entrusted them to Xie Xing Sports Equipment Factory in the city to manufacture. Students of young age in each school are extremely interested in this game. The competition schedule and the rules for mini-football games are recorded below:

(1) Only those who are 58 inches or less in height and weigh 90 pounds or less may participate in the competition. (2) The ball's construction should be around 20 inches to 21 inches in circumference. (The outer layer of the ball should be made of cooked leather, with an air bladder inside, like a football.) (3) The shoes worn during the game should be lightweight soft rubber shoes. Those wearing football shoes will not be allowed to participate in the game. (4) The number of official team members for each game is tentatively set at nine (with unlimited substitutes). (5) The duration of each game is tentatively set at one hour (which can be changed with the agreement of both sides). (6) The dimensions of the football field are tentatively set at 80 yards to 100 yards in length and 60 yards to 80 yards in width. (7) The distance between the two posts of the goal is 7 yards, and the lower edge of the crossbar is 7 feet from the ground. (The width of the center of the post and the depth of the crossbar should be at most 4.5 inches.) (8) The game rules, in addition to slight changes in the size of the field, the number of players, and the length of the game, and other separately stipulated provisions, shall be conducted in accordance with ordinary football rules. (Note) All equipment for this competition, due to time constraints, will not be able to be produced in time and shall be handled in accordance with the environment of each school. (9) The complete schedule is as follows (adopting a double round-robin system, with major and mini-football held on the same day and at the same venue):
